										<p class="menu-bar-popup-title"><a href="/books/content/developmentworkflow-two-approaches-automate-livereloading">Development/Workflow: Two approaches to automate livereloading</a></p>
										<p id="menu-bar-article-one-liner">Since we're working with an interpreted language, which doesn't need to be compiled, the only thing we have to do to make our changes visible, is reloading the page. If you come to a point where you make changes very frequently, you might get annoyed by always reloading it manually. For this reason, we want to have a look at some existing solutions that we can make use of.</p>
